def Stats():
    global users_turn
    global Lv
    global EXP
    global health
    global health_cap
    global punch
    global slash
    global fire_blast

    print("Hp: ",health,"/",health_cap)
    print("Mana: ", mana, "/",mana_cap)
    print("Level: ",Lv)
    print("Exp: ", EXP)
    print("Attacks: ")
    if punch == True:
      print("1) Punch")
    elif slash == True:
      print("2) Slash")
    elif fire_blast == True:
      print("3) Fire Blast")
    print("Turn: ",turn_count)
    users_turn = True

def Move():
    
    print("Where would you like to go?")
    print("North")
    print("South")
    print("East")
    print("Or West")
    global y
    global x

    rsm = ask()
    if rsm == ("north") or rsm == ("North") or rsm == ("up") or rsm == ("Up"):
        y += 1
    elif rsm == ("south") or rsm == ("South") or rsm == ("down") or rsm == ("Down"):
        y -= 1
    elif rsm == ("west") or rsm == ("West") or rsm == ("left") or rsm == ("Left"):
        x -= 1
    elif rsm == ("east") or rsm == ("East") or rsm == ("right") or rsm == ("Right"):
        x += 1
    
    global users_turn
    users_turn = True

def Location():
    print(x,",",y)

    global users_turn
    users_turn = True

def Comands():
  global users_turn
  print(controls)
  users_turn = True
global level_1
level_1 = False
global level_2
level_2 = False
global level_3
level_3 = False
def Level_Check():
  global health_cap
  global mana_cap
  global EXP
  global Lv
  global punch
  global slash
  global fire_blast
  global level_1
  global level_2
  global level_3
  #Check for if the player has already leveled up
  

  if EXP >= 10 and level_1 == False:
    Lv = 1
    level_1 = True
    EXP = EXP - 10
    slash = True
    health_cap = health_cap + 1
    print("Congratsulation on making it to level 1")
    print("You've learned the way of the sword, Slash, unlocked")
    Level_Check()
  elif EXP >= 30 and level_2 == False:
    Lv = 2
    level_2 = True
    EXP = EXP - 30
    fire_blast = True
    health_cap = health_cap + 2
    mana_cap = mana_cap + 1
    print("Welcome to level 2")
    print("You can now feel the magical energy in your soroundings, Fire Ball, unlocked")
    Level_Check()
  elif EXP >= 70 and level_3 == False:
    Lv = 3
    level_3 = True
    EXP = EXP - 70
    health_cap = health_cap + 4
    mana_cap = mana_cap + 2
    print("You made it to level 3, good")
    Level_Check()
global punch
punch = True
global fire_blast
fire_blast = False
global slash
slash = False
def Attack():
    global punch
    global slash
    global mana
    global fire_damage
    global fire_blast
    global damage
    global enemy_crit
    global enemy_crit
    global player_crit
    global criz
    global cicc
    global print_crit
    #Names attacks
    print("What move would you like to use?")
    if punch == True:
        print("1) Punch")
    if slash == True:
        print("2) Slash")
    if fire_blast == True and mana >= 1:
        print("3) Fire Blast")
    #Crit role
    criz = random.randrange(1,17)
    if criz == 16:
      player_crit = True
      criz = 0
    cicc = random.randrange(1,17)
    if cicc == 16:
      enemy_crit = True
      cicc = 0
      

    #Check for if the player has the attack and if its the attack they chose
    rsm = ask()
    if rsm == ("punch") or rsm == ("1") and punch == True:
        damage = random.randrange(1,3)
    if rsm == ("slash") or rsm == ("2") and slash == True:
        damage = random.randrange(3,5)
    if rsm ==("fire blast") or rsm == ("3")and fire_blast == True and mana >= 1:
        fire_damage = True
        damage = random.randrange(2,12)
        mana = mana - 1
    
    if player_crit == True:
      damage = damage * 2
      player_crit = False
      print_crit = True
      Map()
    else:
      Map()
    

def Map():
    global y
    global x
    global harpy1_alive
    global harpy1_health
    global health
    global health_cap
    global mana
    global mana_cap
    global test
    global fish1
    #The players cordnets is set based off of x,y and this is the list of all the places on this grid
    if x == 0 and y == 1:
      clear_output(True)
      print(mountan1_150)
      print("You see a big mountantan looming in the distance. Its so tall you can't even see the top thats hidden completaly in the clouds")
    elif x == 0 and y == 0:
      clear_output(True)
      print(starter_town_150)
      print("This is your home town. You have lived here for many years and know it like the back of your hand")
      print("You feel rejuvinated")
      health = health_cap
      mana = mana_cap
      print("HP:", health,"/",health_cap, " Mana: ", mana, "/", mana_cap)
    elif x == 0 and y == 2 and harpy1_alive == True:
      print("You are attacted...")
      Harpy1()
    elif x == 0 and y == 2 and harpy1_alive == False:
      clear_output(True)
      print("You see a nest in the mountans")
    elif x == 0 and y == -1:
      clear_output(True)
      print(beach1_250)
      print("you feel the drop in air presure as you walk down towards the ocean. You feel a shift in terain as you arive at a beach")
    elif x == 0 and y == -2 and crab1_alive == True:
      clear_output(True)
      print("You are attacked...")
      Crab1()
    elif x == 0 and y == -2:
      print("It's a beach")
    elif x == 1 and y == 0 and test == True:
      Test()
    elif x == 0 and y == -3 and fish1 == True:
      Fish1()


    
    

def Harpy1():
  #The enemy at 0,2 in the mountan area
  global harpy1
  global harpy1_alive
  global harpy1_health
  global damage
  global mana
  global health
  global Dead
  global users_turn
  global health_cap
  global mana_cap
  global EXP
  global enemy_crit
  global print_crit
  #Kills the player if they are less then 0 health
  if health <= 0:
      Dead = True
      users_turn = False
  #Displayes monster's stats
  clear_output(True)
  print(harpy1_150)
  harpy1_health = harpy1_health - damage
  print("You did: ", damage, "damage")
  if print_crit == True:
    print("You got a critical hit!!!!")
    print_hit = False
  damage = 0
  #Prevents the harpy from responing and detects when it dies
  if harpy1_health >= 1:
    harpy1_alive = True
  else:
    clear_output(True)
    print("You have defeted the harpy!")
    EXP = EXP + 5
    damage = 1
    harpy1_alive = False
  dm = random.randrange(1,2)
  if enemy_crit == True:
    dm = dm * 2
    print("You got crit!!!!")
    enemy_crit = False
  print("You took: ", dm, "damage")
  health = health - dm
  print("Harpy's HP:",harpy1_health, "Your HP:", health,"/",health_cap, "Your Mana:", mana,"/",mana_cap)
  if damage == 0 and Dead == False:
    Attack()
  #Ends the program
  damage = 0
  if harpy1_alive == False:
    Map()


def Crab1():
  #If alive v
  global crab1_alive
  #enemy health v
  global crab1_health
  #Global verables v
  global damage
  global mana
  global health
  global Dead
  global users_turn
  global health_cap
  global mana_cap
  global EXP
  global enemy_crit
  global print_crit
  #Kills the player if they are less then 0 health
  if health <= 0:
      Dead = True
      users_turn = False
  #Displayes monster's stats
  clear_output(True)
  #Asky art print v
  print(crab1_150)
  #Damage calc v enemy_health = enemy_health - damage
  crab1_health = crab1_health - damage
  #Displays your damage v
  print("You did: ", damage, "damage")
  #Displays players crit v
  if print_crit == True:
    print("You got a critical hit!!!!")
    print_hit = False
  #Resets damage v
  damage = 0
  #Death detector v
  #If enemy_health v
  if crab1_health >= 1:
    #Alive = True v
    crab1_alive = True
  else:
    #Win senerio
    clear_output(True)
    #Replace enemy with the name of the enemy v
    print("You have defeted the enemy!")
    #Amount of EXP gained EXP = EXP + _
    EXP = EXP + 5
    damage = 1
    #1 = False
    crab1_alive = False
  #Damage of enemy dm = random.randrange(lower number, uper number)
  dm = random.randrange(0,4)
  #Detects enemy's crit
  if enemy_crit == True:
    dm = dm * 2
    print("You got crit!!!!")
    enemy_crit = False
  print("You took: ", dm, "damage")
  #enemy damage on your health calc put defence here
  health = health - dm
  #Diplay for health of enemy print("Harpy's HP:", enemy_health
  print("Crab's HP:",crab1_health , "Your HP:", health,"/",health_cap, "Your Mana:", mana,"/",mana_cap)
  if damage == 0 and Dead == False:
    Attack()
  #Ends the program
  damage = 0
  #enemy_alive == False
  if crab1_alive == False:
    Map()

while(users_turn):
    
    users_turn = False
    turn_count += 1
    
    
    Level_Check()
    
    print("What would you like to do?")
    rsm = ask()
    if rsm == ("stats"):
      Stats()
    elif rsm == ("move"):
      Move()
      Map()
    elif rsm == ("location") or rsm == ("look") or rsm == ("Location"):
      Map()
      Location()
    elif rsm == ("comands") or rsm == ("actions") or rsm == ("inputs") or rsm == ("help") or rsm == ("Help"):
      Comands()
    elif rsm == ("north") or rsm == ("North") or rsm == ("up") or rsm == ("Up"):
      users_turn = True
      y += 1
      Map()
    elif rsm == ("south") or rsm == ("South") or rsm == ("down") or rsm == ("Down"):
      users_turn = True
      y -= 1
      Map()
    elif rsm == ("west") or rsm == ("West") or rsm == ("left") or rsm == ("Left"):
      users_turn = True
      x -= 1
      Map()
    elif rsm == ("east") or rsm == ("East") or rsm == ("right") or rsm == ("Right"):
      users_turn = True
      x += 1
      Map()
